Mayor Wu and Others Initiate the Establishment of the Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association 171

Tuberculosis is a scourge that is most harmful. Mayor Wu, in view of the great success of various countries in organizing anti-tuberculosis groups, initiated the establishment of an anti-tuberculosis association. He has already invited more than 400 people from all walks of life in Shanghai to attend the inaugural meeting at the Municipal Government Reception Center at No. 1881 Xiafei Road at 4:00 PM yesterday. In the future, it will benefit society immeasurably. The origin of the association is recorded as follows: Tuberculosis has been a scourge for a long time, especially in our country. It is estimated that more than 1.2 million Chinese people die from this disease every year, and more than 10 million people are affected. Most of them are young and productive members of society, which has a great impact on the social economy. Fifty years ago, the prevalence of tuberculosis in European and American countries was similar to that in our country. However, due to effective prevention methods, the mortality rate has dropped sharply. For example, in the United Kingdom in 1875, the tuberculosis mortality rate was slightly less than 300 per 100,000, but now it has dropped to about 70, which is clear evidence. Today, the tuberculosis mortality rate in our country, according to surveys, is more than four times that of the United Kingdom, and 40% of children under the age of 14 are infected (according to a report by Gan Yuehan). If active prevention is not taken, how can people's livelihood be imagined? Leaders from all walks of life in Shanghai and doctors have a clearer understanding of the harm of tuberculosis, and have been consulting on prevention methods for a long time. Therefore, they have advocated organizing a national anti-tuberculosis association to actively carry out prevention work, which coincides with the long-standing reputation of Tiecheng. Considering the importance of this matter, it is difficult to achieve results without the masses and the strength of the masses to make step-by-step plans and establish a sound organization. Therefore, we invite talented people from home and abroad to jointly promote its success. We also hope that those who care about people's suffering will be happy to support it. Wu Tiecheng sincerely acknowledges.

The Scene of Sea Lions Jumping Over High Hurdles

Last Saturday, more than 100 people came to Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai express train to see the circus. There were also many people who rushed from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road area. Yesterday morning, a small monkey escaped from the circus, jumping and running, from Gordon Road to Jing'an Temple Road to the intersection of Seymour Road. Passers-by gathered to watch. Later, it broke into the home of a Westerner at No. 99 Seymour Road and fought with a large cat. After the Westerner tried his best to resolve the situation, the monkey was finally captured and taken away by someone from the troupe. There are a total of 250 monkeys in the Haig Bo Circus troupe this time. They devour entire cows, swallowing two in three days, eating and grabbing, without any politeness. It's really interesting.

The Chinese Economic Credit Cooperative is About to Open 177

Zhang Shouyong, Qiu Hanping and others initiate the organization Dr. Qiu Hanping, based on his years of research on cooperative economy and group economy, made detailed plans and initiated the organization of a large-scale economic credit cooperative last winter, named the Chinese Economic Credit Cooperative. Now, the internal preparations are ready, and the Dayang Building at No. 455 Hankou Road has been rented as the cooperative's address. The founding meeting will be held at the end of the month, and the official opening is planned for November 11. The cooperative's operating methods are different from others. Each member of the cooperative not only enjoys the guarantee of savings, life insurance, and dividends, but also has unemployment assistance, various loans, high-quality entertainment, and other economic mutual assistance benefits. Members spend very little, but enjoy a lot. The detailed plan will be announced to the public before the opening, and the significance of the cooperative's organization will be explained to people from all walks of life and the press. Because the founders of the cooperative have always advocated doing more and talking less, no news has been revealed during the preparation period. After its establishment, there will be great plans that will be a mirror for the world.

props were damaged, and the fence was damaged for a total length of 3,619 feet. The most serious damage to trees along the roads was on Yangshupu Road. Special Edition of the Shen Bao National Games No. 12: National Games Closed Yesterday Morning 187

Chairman Lin Personally Presented Awards, All Athletes Fully Rewarded

(Nanjing, 20th dispatch) The National Games held the closing ceremony on the 20th morning at the track and field stadium. The stage was filled with awards, the silver and silk colors extremely dazzling. Around 10 o'clock, Chairman Lin, President Wang, and others arrived successively. Those present included National Government Chairman Lin Sen, Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, Judicial Yuan President Ju Zheng, Legislative Yuan Vice President Shao Yuanzhong, Examination Yuan Vice President Niu Yongjian, Military Council President Tang Shengzhi, Central Guoshu Institute Director Zhang Zhijiang, Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, Minister of Education Wang Shijie, Minister of Transportation Zhu Jiahua, Railway Minister Zeng Zhongming, Nanjing Mayor Shi Ying, National Government Committee members Yang Zhuang, and General Assembly Planning Committee members Chu Minyi, Wang Zhengting, as well as various General Assembly staff, provincial team leaders, athletes, and representatives from various organizations, totaling several thousand people, a grand occasion.

A Glimpse of the Closing Ceremony 188

At 10 o'clock, music started the ceremony. Chairman Lin, President Wang, and other important figures gathered on the eastern stage. The chief team leaders, led by master of ceremonies Xiao Qin, guided the athletes to enter the field in formation, facing the eastern stage. After standing in place, the master of ceremonies shouted, "All stand at attention!" Chairman Wang Shijie led the singing of the Party anthem and three bows, and after reading the will, the chairman delivered the closing speech. Next, Chairman Lin gave an address and presented the awards. Chu Minyi gave a general report on the distribution of prizes, followed by announcing the names one by one, with Chairman Lin personally presenting the awards, which were received by the team leaders representing each team. After the awards were presented, the athlete representative Wang Jihuai gave a response. Then, three cannons were fired and the flag was lowered, completing the ceremony. Music played as everyone dispersed.

The efforts of everyone over the past ten days have suddenly increased the people's confidence in the future of our national revival, and increased a sense of self-confidence. Chairman Lin presenting awards (Nanjing China)

(3) The goal of each athlete is to be non-romantic, non-decadent, and always maintain an optimistic attitude and a spirit of hard work, and to spread this spirit of athletes to Dong Simingtai's prizes (Nanjing China)

The Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee Resolved: The 6th National Games Will Be Held in Shanghai on Double Tenth Festival of the Republic Year 24 191

After Participating in Cooperation between the Far Eastern and Sports Promotion Association, the National Games Will Be Held Every Two Years in Nanjing

(Nanjing, 20th dispatch) After the Ministry of Education established the Physical Education Committee in accordance with the resolutions of the previous National Physical Education Conference, it has held one meeting. The second meeting was held at the Ministry of Education at 4:00 PM on the 20th. More than ten members including Committee Member Wang Zhengting attended. Chu Minyi chaired the meeting. The following resolutions were passed: (1) A proposal to establish physical education supervisors. Please request the Ministry of Education to establish them continuously. (2) A proposal to establish a Central Physical Education Academy. Please request Minister Wang to submit the original proposal to the Executive Yuan meeting again. (3) Determine the name of this year's Games as the 5th National Games. (4) A proposal for the date and location of the 6th National Games. It was resolved that future National Games will be held every two years in Nanjing. However, the 6th National Games will be held in Shanghai due to preparations for the Far Eastern Games venue. The meeting period is set for the Double Tenth Festival of the Republic Year 24. (5) A proposal to participate in next year's Far Eastern Games. It was resolved that this association will cooperate with the Chinese Physical Education Promotion Association. Please request the Promotion Association to draft a plan and budget, which will be transferred by the Ministry of Education to the Executive Yuan for subsidies. (6) A proposal to subsidize the Chinese National Physical Education Promotion Association. It was resolved that the Chinese Physical Education Promotion Association should draft the amount of subsidies required and send it to the Ministry of Education so that it can be requested from the government for subsidies. (7) The proposal for the Chief Training Officer to organize a National Military Physical Education School and the Ministry of Education's proposal to organize a National Physical Education Academy to cooperate with each other was passed. (8) A proposal to continue to hold summer vacation physical education refresher courses next year was passed. Please request the Ministry of Education to organize it.

Speaking of the halberd against Japan, the National Government gave this halberd. Although the item is small, it is hoped that everyone's meaning is great. Today, the conference is closing. I hope that everyone will go back and tell their classmates about the situation of the next conference, what are the strengths and what are the shortcomings, and everyone will continue to work hard in sports until the next conference. When the conference is held, all the young heroes will come again to show off their skills. I wish you all a safe journey home, and I wish you all immeasurable progress in the next conference.

Athlete Representative's Response: Shanghai Team Captain Wang Jihuai 192

At the same time, it shows that the central government attaches importance to sports. During the conference, the result of the efforts of all athletes is that almost all Chinese records have been broken. This is the result of the public's training in sports. If the government and the public work together, then the progress to come is certain. In a few years, it is hoped that Chinese athletes will be on par with all countries in Europe and America.

Qian Xing Su Did Not Violate Competition Rules in Relay Race: National Games Competition Committee Explains Rules 199

(Nanjing, 20th dispatch) The National Games Competition Committee held its fourth meeting at the Ministry of Education at 3:00 PM on the 20th. Twelve people including Zhang Boqin attended. Wang Zhengting chaired the meeting. It was resolved that the Competition Committee meeting on October 8 only explained Article 15 of Chapter 10 of the Competition Rules, and did not amend it. At that time, it was recognized that the women's 400-meter relay was a team event, not an individual event (because the winner of the relay race is the team, not an individual). Therefore, this committee believes that Ms. Qian Xingsu of Shanghai did not violate the provisions of Article 15 of Chapter 10 of the Competition Rules by participating in the 400-meter relay.

Wang Shijie Hosted Banquet for Sports Experts Yesterday 200

(Nanjing, 20th dispatch) Wang Shijie hosted a banquet at the Ministry of Education at noon on the 20th for the sports experts attending this National Games. More than ten people including Chu Minyi, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Boqin, and Yuan Dunli attended. At 2:00 PM, the Central Propaganda Committee screened a silent film of the National Games at the Ministry of Education to entertain the guests. In the film, Wang Jingwei's speech, Chu Minyi leading elementary school students in Beijing in performing Tai Chi exercises, and Chu's personal performance of knife and stick skills were all spirited and lively. At 7:00 PM, Lianhua Company screened a sound film of the National Games at the Ministry of Education, inviting experts attending the National Games, with many attendees.

Final Scene of the Games 201

(Nanjing, 20th dispatch) The following are some situations after the closing of the National Games, which are worth telling to the readers, and are recorded in a miscellaneous way to mark the end.

(1) Encirclement for Lin and Wang's Signatures 202

After the closing of the National Games at noon on the 20th, Lin Sen, Wang Qingwei, Wang Shijie, Zhang Boqin, and Wang Zhengting were surrounded by athletes who requested signatures on their handbooks to keep as souvenirs. Wang signed (Work hard and strive), (Strive to be strong), (Wish you progress) and other words. At that time, there were many athletes, and Wang, Lin, and others signed one by one. After being surrounded for half an hour, Wang and others were able to escape. In the afternoon, Wang and Zeng Zhongming and others held a meeting in the field to welcome the Guangdong delegation. Wang and others each gave speeches, and dispersed after a while.

(2) Tidying Up Luggage One After Another 203

With the end of the National Games, which had been extremely grand, the athletes from various units tidied up their luggage one after another and set off separately. Inside and outside the front and rear gates of the General Assembly, luggage boxes and cages were piled up like mountains. Male and female athletes either carried scattered items or waited for the bus to depart. Those who triumphed held prizes in their hands, looking triumphant and proud, while those who failed looked sideways, looking quite frustrated. However, the prizes were huge and packed in wooden boxes due to time constraints, so they could not be done, so they were all carried with them. In addition, books, newspapers, etc. donated by various parties were bundled up, and everyone found it difficult to carry them. Yang Xiuhuan, the first choice for women's swimming in Hong Kong, wore a long crimson cheongsam, and Wang Fengjing and Wang Chunyuan, the first choices for women's tennis, wore white vests, white shoes and socks, with unparalleled charm. They attracted the most attention from the audience when they received awards.

(3) Departure Dates of Each Team 204

The departure dates of each team, as far as is known from the investigation, are recorded as follows: Zhejiang and Suiyuan set off on the evening of the 18th, and Gansu and Jiangxi left Beijing on the afternoon of the 19th. Teams from Jiangsu, Anhui, Shanghai, and Northeast China left Beijing on the morning of the 20th. Teams from Henan, Hebei, Shandong, and Shanxi set off in the afternoon of the 20th, taking the 5:00 PM special train on the Jinpu Railway back north. Teams from Fujian and Guizhou took the evening train to Shanghai. Teams from Hubei and Hunan, who left Beijing on the morning of the 21st, all took the Jiangshun Wheel west. The Sichuan team took the early train to Shanghai to visit on the 28th, and then took the Minsheng Company's Minshun Wheel back to Sichuan. Teams from Hong Kong, Guangdong, and Yunnan took the early train to Shanghai. The Qingdao team took the early train back north via the Jinpu Railway. In addition, the Philippine and Brazilian teams, due to the small number of people, all went to the Overseas Chinese Guest House and left one after another.

(4) Considerable Shipping Costs for Prizes 205

The prizes for the women's overall championship were temporarily stored at the General Assembly because the Guangdong team requested the General Assembly to retain them for the second time. After the competition committee resolves the issue, they will be claimed. This time, almost all of the men's and women's track and field ball championships were won by the Shanghai team. Most of the prizes arranged on the stage should be claimed by the Shanghai team. However, the number is very large, so the Shanghai team specially left Shao Rugan in Beijing to ask China Travel Service to pack them in boxes. It is heard that the shipping cost alone will cost hundreds of yuan.

(5) Closing of the General Assembly Office 206

Except for the General Affairs, Reception, and Transportation Groups, whose affairs were busy and continued to work as usual, the furniture and items in the Propaganda and Documents Groups' offices were moved out in the afternoon, leaving only one or two people stationed at the conference to manage them. Each section of the Competition Committee retained three cadres to stay at the conference because the conference affairs had been completed.

(6) Temporary Shops Closing 207

Except for a few food stores, which continued to operate as usual, the remaining large and small shopping malls at the General Assembly were completely closed in the afternoon. It is heard that the most developed businesses were the food stores. Within ten days, they were all full of people and extremely crowded. Now that people have left and the building is empty, I can't help but feel the contrast between the past and the present when I step on the ground. Secondly, the business of fruits and candies was also prosperous. According to the Fu Ronghe fruit stall, it made more than 1,000 yuan in business in ten days, making a considerable profit.

(7) Guangdong-Hong Kong Buji Football 208

The Guangdong-Hong Kong mixed football team is scheduled to compete with the Shanghai team at the Zhonghua Stadium on the afternoons of the 21st and 23rd. At 3:00 PM on the 22nd, the Hong Kong-Shanghai Chinese football Buji match will be held. The Hong Kong team will be represented by the South China Athletic Association football team, and will compete against the Shanghai team participating in the National Games. On the afternoon of the 24th, the Hong Kong football champion South China team will compete against the Shanghai football league champion Donghua team. In addition, Guangdong male swimmers are scheduled to compete against Shanghai Western swimmers on the 21st and 23rd.

(8) The Shi Family Army Will Return to Liaoning 209

Liaoning swimming athletes Shi Xingxi and Xinglu and their younger sister have not yet left Beijing. Soon, they will hold a Yangtze River swimming event with their eldest brother Shi Xinglong. Shi said that the Beijing municipal government does not allow assistance. I am determined to wait for a sunny day to take my younger brother and weaker sister to do this swimming, and take the opportunity to travel south. The four of them will go to Shanghai for a visit, and then return to Liaoning from Shanghai.

(9) Not Everything Can Be Satisfactory 210

After the meeting, a member of the organizing committee talked about the fact that not everything in this National Games was satisfactory, which has been criticized by public opinion. The propaganda team originally scheduled to host a banquet for the partners on the 21st, but it has now been cancelled. However, the weather was sunny during the meeting, and the General Assembly had the advantage of the weather, which is something that human power cannot do. The excellent results of the competition are gratifying.

(10) Reporters Are Not Included 211

In the closing speech of the Chairman Wang Shijie, he expressed his gratitude to everyone from the organizing committee down to the Boy Scouts, but he did not mention a single word about the efforts of various newspapers to expand their coverage and diligently record the events. Recalling the closing remarks of Cai Yuanpei, Jiang Menglin, and Zhu Jiahua at the Third National Education Conference and the National Physical Education Conference last year, they expressed sincere gratitude for the efforts of the news reporters. This is the difference in the speech.

National Martial Arts Examination Opened Yesterday Morning 212

(Nanjing, 20th, Central News Agency) The second National Martial Arts Examination, organized by the Central Martial Arts Academy, held its opening ceremony at 8:00 AM on the 20th. Attendees included Chairman Lin, Central Representative Chu Minyi, Committee Member Jiang's representative Cao Haosen, Central Committee members Zhang Ji, Jiao Yitang, Ding Chaowu, Li Liejun, Wang Zhengting, Shi Ying, and Niu Yongjian, Li Yuanding, Zhang Bocen, Lü Chao, Lai Lian, Director of the Martial Arts Academy Zhang Zhijiang, all referees and athletes, totaling over two thousand people. Chairman Zhang Zhijiang delivered the opening address, reporting on the preparations for this National Examination and its important significance, stating briefly that in this time of strong enemies pressing our borders and serious national crisis, we should promote the spirit of martial arts to save us from danger and destruction. Following him, Chu Minyi, Chairman Lin, Cao Haosen, Niu Yongjian, Li Liejun, and others delivered speeches in succession, offering encouragement to all athletes. Next, all referees and athletes took an oath. Immediately afterward, the Martial Arts Anthem was sung, its melodious and inspiring rhythm exuding a spirit of vigorous and flourishing progress. Then, the ceremony concluded and the meeting adjourned. In the afternoon, there were group performances and preliminary tests of boxing techniques. (Nanjing, 20th) The second National Martial Arts Examination held its opening ceremony at the Public Stadium on the morning of the 20th. Chairman Lin personally attended and delivered an exhortation. Committee Member Jiang, due to the urgency of suppressing bandits at the front, could not spare himself, so he specially dispatched Army Deputy Cao Haosen as his representative to attend and deliver a speech. In the afternoon, students from the Central Political School demonstrated boxing techniques, students from Jinling Middle School demonstrated saber techniques in preliminary tests. Students from the Martial Arts Academy performed Shaolin boxing, and preliminary tests for athletes were also held. They were divided into ten groups, with items including saber, spear, staff, boxing, sword, and halberd. In addition, each athlete added one item. Sixty points was passing, eighty points was standard, and one hundred points was full marks. Those below sixty points were not allowed to participate in the official competition. The competition started on the 21st, and the entrance ticket price was changed to two jiao.

He Jian Sends Representatives to Participate (Nanjing, 20th, Central News Agency) The National Martial Arts Examination held its opening ceremony on the 20th. He Jian sent Li Liju, Xiang Kairan, Wan Tianshi, Zhu Guozhen, Tang Chonglie, and Guo Shixian to participate as representatives. The Hunan athletes, totaling over a hundred people, were neatly dressed and in high spirits, earning praise from the audience. The National Examination Assembly hired Li Liju as a referee committee member, Xiang Kairan as an advisor, and Wan Tianshi, Zhu Guozhen, Guo Shixian, Tang Chonglie, Wu Gongzao, and Song Ruifeng as assistant referee committee members to assist in presiding over the refereeing matters. He Jian sent a telegram from Hunan, planning to come to Nanjing to participate immediately after finishing the affairs in Nanchang.

Opening Ceremony of the National Examination (Nanjing Zhonghua)

Amidst Thunderous Cheers, the Iron Army of This City Returns to Shanghai in Triumph. Mayor Wu Greets and Encourages the Athletes at the Station. A Parade Will Depart from the City Center This Afternoon. 213

The National Games concluded yesterday. The athletes of this city worked hard, did not disgrace their mission, and returned with the overall championships for both men and women. The first batch of staff and athletes of the city delegation, one hundred and eighty people led by Chen Bai, left Beijing at 8:00 AM yesterday morning and arrived at 2:20 PM. Mayor Wu and representatives from various groups and schools welcomed them at the station. The second batch of athletes, including Wang Jihuai and more than ten others, loaded with prizes, left Beijing on the 5:25 PM train and also arrived in Shanghai at 11:50 PM last night. The details are recorded as follows:

Representatives from All Circles Welcome at the Station 214

Those who came to welcome at the station yesterday included Mayor Wu, Director Pan, Director Wen, Zhang Tingrong from the municipal government, Tong Muge, Yu Zhongbiao, and Pei Zi from the municipal party headquarters, Zhou Feicheng and Ma Chonggan from the municipal education bureau, Huang Zaoxiong from the municipal education association, Xie Yandu leading all the Boy Scouts of the 121st Regiment as representatives of the municipal Boy Scout Council, Yang Dean from the University Federation, as well as representatives from Youyou Sports Association, Donghua Sports Association, Lufeng Bookstore, Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, and thousands of students from Fudan University, Jinan University, Southeast Women's Physical Education School, Liangjiang Physical Education College, Dongya Physical Education College, Wuben Girls' Middle School, Dazhong Middle School, Dagong Vocational School, and the municipal Yude, Feihong, and He'an First Kindergarten.

Enthusiastic Scene at the Train Station 215

The welcoming personnel gathered at 2:00 PM. The train station was crowded with people and fluttering flags. The Municipal Public Security Bureau specially dispatched a military band to the station to play welcoming music. All the patrolmen from the five district branches were on duty to maintain order. Various institutions and groups held white welcome flags with inscriptions such as "Welcome athletes participating in the National Games," or "Welcome Shanghai team athletes winning the championship," or "Celebrate Shanghai team winning the championship, long live success," in bright colors and varied styles. The students from each school held small flags with warning slogans such as "This is called the gentleman's competition" and "From the sports field to the international battlefield," the words of which were particularly humorous.

Athletes Arrive, Cheers Thunder 216

The train arrived at the North Train Station at 2:20 PM amidst the resounding music of the military band and the crackling of firecrackers. The train car assigned to the athletes was number 452. When it arrived at the station, all the welcoming personnel took off their hats, raised their flags, and applauded thunderously. All the athletes leaned on the windows, smiling and expressing their gratitude. Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and others shook hands with the athletes one by one to express their joy. The situation was enthusiastic, truly unprecedented. At 2:50 PM, the welcoming teams and athletes began to leave the platform in an orderly fashion.

Mayor's Speech Encourages Athletes 217

The athletes then gathered in the open space outside the station, where Mayor Wu delivered a speech, stating briefly: "Today, we welcome you back in triumph in the name of Shanghai. The Shanghai team athletes, after ten days of hard work, running around, and striving hard, finally won the overall championships for both men and women in this National Games. This is not only the glory of Shanghai, but also the glory of the citizens of Shanghai and your parents, relatives, and friends. The fate of the Republic of China depends entirely on the youth. Your efforts are not just personal efforts, but represent the efforts of the entire Republic of China. I hope you will continue to forge ahead, temper your physique, and predict that in the future at the Far Eastern Games, and even the World Games, you will also be able to win championships and return. Only then will there be a bright future for China." Director Pan then delivered a welcome speech, with many words of encouragement. Immediately afterward, the Municipal Education Bureau prepared four large trucks to send the athletes back to their schools along different routes.

Second Batch of Athletes Returned to Shanghai Last Night 218

The second batch of athletes, including Wang Jihuai and about ten other staff members, left Beijing on the 5:25 PM train after attending the closing ceremony to receive awards. They arrived in Shanghai at 11:50 PM last night, loaded with prizes from the conference. Representatives from the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Public Security Bureau Military Band were all present at the station to welcome them.

Grand Banquet at the New City Hall This Afternoon 219

The Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government have scheduled a banquet at 12:30 PM today at the new City Hall in the city center to celebrate the participation of all staff and athletes in the National Games. They have also sent invitations to the Garrison Headquarters, as well as the heads and leaders of various municipal organs, newspaper offices, and social groups. In terms of transportation, three large trucks have been prepared at the end of the shooting range road in Hongkou Park, across from the outdoor swimming pool of the Public Works Department, to shuttle back and forth from 10:30 AM to 12:30 PM. All staff and athletes participating in the National Games must wear uniforms, and staff must wear white pants. Each team should bring a small team flag for photography and parade purposes.

Entire Team of Athletes to Parade This Afternoon 220

Clothing Special Issue, Seventh Issue. True Beauty of Clothing 231

What standard do we use to judge the beauty of clothing? I think we can only distinguish it based on truth and falsehood. What is true beauty? In terms of material, domestically produced clothing material is true beauty. In terms of color, simple and non-fading clothing material is true beauty. In terms of style, elegant and practical clothing material is true beauty. In terms of economy, cheap, durable, and wear-resistant clothing material is true beauty. In general, only by wearing truly beautiful clothing can one receive respect and admiration from others. If one wears foreign labels, foreign silk crepe, or foreign wool, then one has lost true beauty. The English Queen wore Lancashire cotton cloth and was respected by the entire nation, almost to the point of becoming a trend. The whole nation followed suit, considering wearing this kind of clothing the supreme glory of life, much more noble than embroidered dragon and phoenix brocade and luxurious clothing. This is because clothing made of domestic cloth meets the standards of true beauty. Extending this further, Meiya's silk crepe, Zhanghua's wool, and Hongxin's fabrics are all leaders of domestic goods, truly equal in status and with their own true value. However, in recent times, morality has declined, with falsehoods replacing truths, and deceptive tricks emerging endlessly, making it difficult for those who love to wear beautiful clothing to distinguish between them. First, materials that are clearly inferior foreign goods are disguised, causing genuine domestic silk crepe, domestic wool, and domestic fabrics to lose their position in sales. Second, colors should gain the trust of customers by not fading, but currently, fading clothing material is everywhere. This indeed kills the enthusiasm of those who love to use domestic goods. Manager Xu Yangnan of Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory once said, "The morality of clothing lies in not fading." This is very true. Third, in terms of style, it also follows the trend of colors. If there is elegant and non-fading clothing material, making clothing will naturally be fitting and beautiful, and people will naturally flock to it. This is obvious. Fourth, in terms of economy, in this year of domestic goods and the era of everyone enjoying domestic goods, the only obligation of producers is to make small profits and sell more, and to reduce costs. If they take this opportunity to raise prices, they are inviting failure. Even those who love to use domestic goods will retreat three times. Moreover, in terms of products, they should not only be cheap but also durable and wear-resistant, so that the true beauty of clothing can be maintained forever.

Truly beautiful clothing, lovely truly beautiful clothing, I hope manufacturers who pay attention to clothing will satisfy the desire to use domestic goods.

Tea No Clothes

Winter Clothes King 232

(Autumn harvest and winter storage) This old saying refers to the Chinese habit of thousands of years, because all agricultural products are generally harvested abundantly in autumn, and stored in winter, which can be used for a year's use. So in winter, business is very prosperous, and there are especially many folk marriages, so the shops selling clothing fabrics, business is particularly prosperous.

However, in Shanghai, and the ports close to Shanghai, most people generally buy more clothes in summer and autumn, because the clothing fabrics in summer and autumn are relatively cheaper, so they see the clothes fabrics they love, but buy them at any time, make clothes at any time, but did not budget for the cost of winter clothing fabrics, and when winter comes, they have no ability to buy more.

In fact, winter clothing fabrics are extremely needed, and winter clothing, if it should be added but not added, will feel shabby. Now society only values clothing, not human feelings, so the cost of household mourning clothing should have a budget throughout the year, in the summer and autumn rainy season, in addition to the indispensable, must not be too wasteful, must not be willfully added, and for winter clothing, should be added to add, do not hesitate.

Editor's Report on This Month's Clothing Style Changes 233

In addition to the ever-changing fashion styles, which are not easy to explain, in this month, the clothing styles for men and women in Shanghai have gradually changed compared with last month, now roughly reported as left ··

Women's clothing fabrics, the lightest color is orange, the deepest is blue and coffee ·, men's clothing fabrics, the most popular color is blue and ink gray.

The hem of the women's cheongsam is gradually wider than before ·, and the length of the clothes has gradually decreased, at most one foot and two inches, and the lowest is only eight inches. The clothes are all lined with mink edges ·, or very wide satin rolls, and the light-colored lines embedded in the rolls are absolutely not popular. The buttons on the placket are usually nailed with three ordinary straight walnut knots, and no one consults the spiral incense buttons and loop buttons. Although the lining of the clip cheongsam is not connected to the hem of the robe, but those decorated with lace are gradually less seen.

Men's robes, whether lined with velvet clip robes, are no longer popular for making patches, and the collar has gradually decreased a little ·, and there are also many people with a roll of one side inlaid on the four edges of the vest ·, but it has not yet become popular.

Mourning Spinning Mill Combing Workshop

Studies on Clothing and Environment: Considerations for Color Tone, Style, Age, and Figure 236

The color tone of women's clothing is most closely related to age and figure. As for the material of the clothing, whether it is silk, cloth, or wool, it is all the same. When we go out on the streets of Shanghai, we often see the backs of many women without being able to see their faces. Almost all of them are young women of eighteen or nineteen years of age. However, if the color tones of their clothes are used inappropriately, it can often increase dislike, so it is of great value to study.

Generally speaking, the most taboo thing for overweight people in clothing is large patterns. Deep red and bright green are also unsuitable. It is best to choose lighter colors, or small willow-shaped or long-shaped patterns, which can make others seem to perceive a reduction in their weight. This is a kind of illusion in psychology. Short people should also use willow-shaped long patterns.

However, this cannot be generalized. If a woman is over thirty and is short and plump, she should definitely not use delicate colors, but should use neutral colors.

Ordinary people believe that women with fair complexions can make their fair faces appear even whiter by wearing black or dark-colored clothing. However, reality and ideals are often inversely proportional. We only need to pay attention to Western women. Their skin color is very fair. Except for mourning days, winter, or old age, they rarely use dark or black colors, because the matching of color tones must seek neutrality to feel harmonious and comfortable. Savage nations mostly like stimulating color tones. In addition, only prostitutes are like this. In civilized cities, stimulating colors are rarely piled on them. Therefore, the fairer a woman's complexion is, the more suitable she is to use neutral-colored clothing, and the patterns on the clothing should be regular but not very obvious, so as not to feel fiery.

The beauty of clothing can certainly increase a person's beauty, but the women's clothing in Shanghai is too generally prostitute-like, and the prostitutes are also generally good-family-woman-like. This is a very worrying thing. They have completely disregarded their own age, identity, and figure, and single-mindedly want to become or force themselves into being a budding young girl, or even a girl who can captivate the masses, desperately working hard in terms of clothing and makeup. As a result, the result is the opposite. You must know that the beauty of women is certainly the most beautiful around the age of twenty, but around the age of thirty, or even around the age of forty, if the clothing is appropriate, it is enough to show the beauty suitable for her age. If you want to pretend to be seventeen or eighteen years old, it will definitely be like painting a tiger and failing, resembling a dog instead.

Therefore, once past middle age, one should tend towards simplicity, and around the age of twenty, one should also consider one's own skin color and figure to match appropriate clothing. The fashions that have been popular recently are mostly evolved from Western-style clothing. For example, people with thick waists can add a few frills on both sides of the lower waist of the clothes, which can make people hallucinate that her waist is large and not feel that her waist is thick. Also, people with dark upper arms can make dark-colored lantern-style short sleeves, which can also reduce the ugliness of thick, dark arms.

Tall, thin people should not use willow-shaped or long-shaped patterned fabrics. Short, fat people should not use round flower patterns. People with short legs should not use red-like colors. People with a lot of hair should not use black or brown. These are very obvious and easy to know.

Chinese women also have a habit of liking several sisters, or several close acquaintances, to dress completely alike, or seeing others cut a piece of fabric and make a fashionable dress, they will imitate it in the same way, without studying whether it is suitable for them to wear. If they put it on and feel it doesn't look good, but discard it, this is also very related to economic aspects. Therefore, each person has their own suitable clothing, there is no need to imitate others, this is the first essential of studying clothing, blindly following others will definitely not get praise from others, and their own satisfaction.

Wireless Weekly

High-Frequency Amplification in Transmitters 237

— Ming Xiang

Modern broadcasting or signal transmitters, in addition to the main oscillation stage, have at least one or more stages of high-frequency amplification. The most important thing in the high-frequency amplification stage is the neutralization device, unless the vacuum tube used is a screen-grid type. The purpose of neutralization is to avoid self-oscillation of the vacuum tube due to the coupling of the internal capacitance of the vacuum tube, which interferes with the frequency stimulated by the oscillation stage and loses its amplification effect, which is the same as the high-frequency stage of a radio.

Vacuum tubes used for high-frequency amplification are usually Class B amplification. Its grid negative potential is extremely high. When there is no excitation, the grid current is actually equal to zero. The reason for using Class B amplification instead of the usual Class A or audio frequency amplification is that the efficiency of Class A amplification is only 15%, while Class B can get 80 to 85%. The diagram shows a simple oscillation amplification transmitter amplification stage circuit. The high-frequency electrical energy output from the oscillation stage is fed to the input circuit of the amplification stage through the coupling capacitor C2 via the feeder lines A and B. Because there is a high-frequency choke RFO connected across, the high-frequency current cannot flow into the C battery circuit, otherwise it will be a loss. To test whether this choke is reliable, simply connect a bypass capacitor C4, as shown by the dotted line. If the screen-grid current does not change when connected, it proves that this choke is perfect and reliable, otherwise, it has failed.

The ammeter and C battery in series in the grid circuit are very valuable indicators. After the oscillation and amplification stages are turned on, this meter will have an index indicating the corresponding value of the excitation voltage, so its function is actually equal to a high-frequency voltage meter, which is very helpful in the neutralization amplification stage. The direct current flowing through this grid current meter is the direct current after the high-frequency voltage is rectified by the grid of the amplification tube. This point must be clearly understood. (To be continued)

Sand Noise in Dynamic Loudspeakers 238

— Yi Zhi

When a dynamic loudspeaker on an AC machine has sand noise, the tone becomes complex and vague, and unpleasant to the ear. There are approximately three reasons for this annoying sand noise:

(1) Rust on the poles of the electromagnet. There is a huge electromagnet inside the dynamic loudspeaker (if readers want to know the simple principle and structure of the dynamic loudspeaker, please refer to my article (Talking about Loudspeakers), published in this journal on July 8). Due to moisture intrusion and long-term disuse, the poles of this magnet rust, forming a thin layer of iron filings. When the voice coil vibrates, it rubs against it and generates irregular motion, causing sand noise. The repair method is to carefully disassemble the loudspeaker, wipe it clean with fine sandpaper (used to wipe the commutator on the generator), or wipe it clean with cotton dipped in kerosene, and then apply a little oil and wipe it dry with a cloth, so that it is not easy to rust in the future.

(2) Dust and sand accumulate between the electromagnet and the voice coil. The gap between the mother magnetic field electromagnet and the voice coil is approximately one-thousandth to fifteen-thousandths of an inch, so dust and sand accumulate in it. When the voice coil vibrates, it can rub and cause sand noise. This dust and sand is easier to remove. Sometimes, inverting the loudspeaker and waiting for it to vibrate violently a few times will allow the dust and sand to fall out naturally.

(3) Loose screws and other reasons. If the screws on the loudspeaker are loose, the electromagnet may come into contact with the voice coil after vibration. When the voice coil vibrates, sand noise caused by friction occurs. Sometimes, the voice coil may also develop this problem due to poor construction, dampness, or skew. The repair method is to correct the voice coil so that it does not contact the magnet, and place it in a ventilated place to dry it.

In short, a good dynamic loudspeaker will never emit unpleasant sand noise. The occurrence of sand noise must be due to the voice coil coming into contact with the electromagnet or dust and sand during vibration, causing friction. To protect the dynamic loudspeaker from emitting sand noise, it should be placed in a clean and dry place to avoid the trouble of repair.

Remedies for Unstable Voltage 239

— Wei Xin Su

Power supply in the mainland often has unstable voltage, especially when the lights are lit up at dusk, and during special festivals, due to insufficient current supply, the voltage drops, which greatly affects the use of AC radios. Conversely, if the current consumption decreases, there is often an excessive voltage, which makes the radio even more dangerous. The remedy is to add a step-down transformer in front of the primary stage of the radio power square shed, as shown in the figure above. This square shed can be filled with an electric bell shed. There is a kind on the market with primary IIOV and secondary 2.5, 3V, 5V, 7, 9V, etc., which is very suitable for needs.

For example, if the voltage in Area A drops by 5V at dusk, then put S on the 5V terminal. In this way, the output voltage of the secondary stage of the step-down square shed is 5V. Because it is connected in series with the input circuit of the radio power square shed, according to the principle of (if the positive terminal of Voltage A is connected in series with the negative terminal of Voltage B, then the total voltage equals Voltage A plus Voltage B), it can compensate for the drop of 5V. If there is excessive voltage, a double-pole double-throw switch can be used to invert the primary stage terminal of the small square shed to change the electrode of its secondary output, and use the neutralization principle to cancel the small square shed output voltage with the radio power square shed input voltage, then (the total voltage equals Voltage A minus Voltage B).

Directionality of Large Antennas (Continued) 240

— Jin

The above is the situation when viewed from above, that is, when the antenna transmits and receives in all directions of the horizon. Now, if you observe in the direction of the horizon, and see the situation of the antenna transmitting and receiving in the vertical direction, it is different again. The situation of the simplest vertical antenna can be seen in the second figure. From that curve, we can know that the direction with the greatest transmitting and receiving ability is in the horizontal direction, that is, the direction with zero degrees with the horizontal. The larger the angle with the horizontal, the weaker the transmitting and receiving ability. For example, the ability to 25 degrees, represented by Gb, is only half of Ga at 0 degrees. The larger the angle, the smaller the transmitting and receiving ability, and after 50, it is almost gone. Therefore, this type of antenna cannot communicate with airplanes. However, if you use the inverted L type, the lead-in wire of that antenna is equivalent to a vertical antenna. Now that the flat top part has the maximum transmitting and receiving ability only in the direction of the sky and the earth. Except for the refraction effect, it has almost no transmitting and receiving ability on the horizontal aspect, so at this time, the vertical lead-in wire is just responsible for transmitting and receiving on the horizontal ground. Therefore, this type of antenna has great transmitting and receiving ability in both the horizontal and vertical directions. The other TV types are the same.

The directionality mentioned above can be very useful. The figure below is the most convenient way to use it. This is the best device when both transmitting and receiving antennas use the inverted L type. That is to say, the two are in the same plane, and the grounded ends are installed close to each other head to head. When the ordinary radio is receiving, pointing the inverted L antenna at the transmitting station, and connecting the grounded end in the direction of the transmitting station, will make the receiving result like a point, which is why. However, it should be noted that if you use a very short antenna, this kind of directionality is not very obvious. If the flat top part is longer and installed lower, this kind of directionality is more obvious. (End)

Self-Made Tester Ammeter Li Yuanqing 241

—

Using a voltmeter in series with a battery to test whether various radio parts are damaged is the simplest and most accurate method. However, the sensitivity of the voltmeter used for this test must be as high as possible, otherwise it will feel impractical when testing.

The price of a voltmeter with reliable sensitivity is very expensive. It is inevitable for ordinary radio enthusiasts to feel quite difficult to purchase one. This article specifically introduces a tester ammeter with a simple structure for readers to use. As shown in the figure, first wind 1,000 to 2,000 turns of No. 36 enameled wire on a coil frame made of thick cardboard (the more turns, the more sensitive the effect). After winding, use copper sheet to fix the coil on the wooden board. (In the figure, a corner of the copper sheet is missing to show the winding method of the coil.) Then embed an ordinary military-use pocket compass in one end of the coil frame, and clamp the other end with copper sheet. The battery in series can be placed on the table or hidden under the board. Then move the wooden board, wait until the compass is at a right angle to the coil (as shown in the figure), and then you can use it.

For example, if you want to test a transformer, you only need to connect the wire ends to the two stacks of A and B in turn, and see if the compass moves to find out where the broken wire or short circuit is.

Although the above-mentioned tester ammeter has a very simple structure, its effect is exceptionally sensitive. When half a milliampere passes through the coil, the pointer can jump. This point is beyond the reach of any other cheap voltmeter. (Note: Even the smallest screw in this voltmeter must not use magnetized materials such as steel and iron, otherwise the magnetic needle will lose its effect.)

Casual Chat after Listening (1) 242

— Wei Yan

The Current Situation of Domestic Broadcasting

Among all the broadcasting stations in China, the Nanjing Central Broadcasting Station is the largest in terms of power. In terms of quantity, Shanghai is the most. Now, let’s briefly describe the broadcasting programs of these two stations. The broadcasting stations in other places will be discussed later.

Nanjing

Before the Nanjing Central Broadcasting Station (XGOA) was renovated with large machines, the programs were not as rich as they are now. Except for lectures, news, records, and at most once a week special programs (national opera, Kunqu opera, etc.), there is nothing else worth mentioning. When the station tested a 75,000-watt transmitter last summer, the author sent a letter requesting to add the following types of programs:

(1) Increase various academic programs (teaching Chinese, etc.) to educationalize the broadcasting industry.

(2) Add programs on radio knowledge and Q&A to instill radio knowledge to the general public and solve the difficulties encountered by listeners during experimentation.

(3) Add more entertainment programs to arouse public interest in radio.

After the station officially opened on the birthday of the Premier last year, it made major adjustments to the programs. In addition to the above-mentioned points, which have been added one after another, it has also added code practice, commercial intelligence reports, and national martial arts morning exercises programs, which were temporarily full of pleasant sounds.

The efforts of the Central Broadcasting Station to collect programs are indeed higher than the hopes of ordinary people. The past facts can prove that:

(1) Experts were specially invited to compile several volumes of drum lyrics, such as Sun Yat-sen's London escape, Qiu Jin's martyrdom, and signing a false contract to sell out, etc., and invited drum masters He Zhichen, Jin Yufang, etc. to take turns to play and sing on the stage, which was very popular among the audience.

(2) Schools, groups, and amateur opera troupes in Beijing have been played by the station almost all over. Famous actors such as Cheng Yanqiu, Xin Yanqiu, and Xu Biyun have all broadcasted on the station successively. When it opened last winter, Mei Lanfang was invited to participate, although it could not be realized due to the matter, but the station's concern for collecting programs can be seen.

Small Experience Soldering Method of Earphone Lead Wire 243

— Li Yuanqing

The lead wire of ordinary earphones or speakers is most likely to be detached from the copper feet (Tip) after long-term use. Sometimes, even if it is not detached, the inside has already loosened. Therefore, it is inconvenient to use or it is often easy to cause noise. The only way to remedy it is to disassemble it and solder it again.

We know that it is most difficult to solder lead wires whose outer surface is plated with metal (see issue 21 of this journal). Sometimes the solder has not melted, but the wire has already been charred, especially inside the copper feet, which makes you sigh that your arms are too short to reach!

The method introduced in this article can relieve you of this difficulty. First, use a knife to cut off the insulation on the outside of the wire (about one inch), and then wrap a thin copper wire tightly around the lead wire. Then stuff a little solder into the copper feet (the inside of the copper feet should be cleaned first). Finally, clamp the copper feet with pliers and put them on a spirit lamp to burn. After the solder inside is completely dissolved, insert the lead wire with a knife, and it will be as strong as before after standing cold for one minute. (Note: The lead wire and the inside of the copper feet must be pre-coated with solder flux before soldering.)

Self-Made Small Light Bulb Holder 244

— Yun

It can be made with two nails, a small piece of wood or hard thick paper, and a section of useless thick copper wire. It seems worthless, but its use is very great, such as for protecting filaments, illuminating dials, and testing circuits. The manufacturing method is as shown in the figure. Wrap a section of about No. 14 thick bare copper wire around a penholder for four or five turns, and nail one end to the paper with a long nail. Nail another nail in the center under the circle. Calculate the distance between the two nails so that they can be inserted into the vacuum tube socket to test whether the voltage of the filament is accurate.

Views on Death 245

— Qing Qu

People often say (view of life), thinking that there is a (meaning) as a guise. But I don’t know that after talking about it, there is still no meaning, because since a person has been made, in this kind of net and shackles, it is like being in the realm of five turbidities, how can he jump out of the Asura’s field, and everyone goes to climb the Avatamsaka dream (Golden World) (Pure Land)? You! If you don’t believe it, try to look at Peter the Great, who was famous in history, although he is dead and buried in the imperial mausoleum, hey! After a hundred years, his silver coffin will turn over, and all the funeral treasures will be unearthed and sold by the living, isn’t it a significant cause and effect that no matter how heroic he was in his life, he is still unreliable after death? Let’s not talk about the remote examples, let’s take the present as an example. Chen Jiongming of Guangdong is dead, and his (rights and wrongs, merits and demerits) will be recorded in the future history, so we don’t need to criticize him. However, he died, and he ended up with a reputation of desolation and no possessions outside of himself. Old Wu’s words can really awaken the delusions of many people, especially in (views on death), and under the definition, if it is not the case, it is (making children and grandchildren as opium addicts, as playboys), alas! I don’t know that the world is like cattle and horses who have been sons and grandsons before they were born, seeking fields and houses, and busy for a lifetime, but they have not enjoyed any happiness. When the moment of death comes, breathing stops, and hearing and vision also stop, those who talk long and short will have to estimate how much property he left behind. In fact, except for his children, no one else can share anything, and it has become a custom. A few days ago, Wu Yiqing in our county) died in Shanghai, and someone said that he (had no savings after his death and felt pity), I heard that this old man used to be a minister to Italy and was also an official, but he had no money after his death, which is his noble character, not insulting the people of our county. If you misunderstand this point, you have not died thoroughly to the essence of (views on death)!

National Product Champagne 246

— Rong Yu

Auspicious words of praise and blessing are so pleasing to the ear. On the first day of the New Year, people shout "Congratulations and may you be prosperous!" When seeing someone off, they say "Smooth sailing!" To congratulate newlyweds, "May your home be harmonious and prosperous with many children and grandchildren!" To wish someone a birthday, "May your fortune be as vast as the East Sea and your life as long as the Southern Mountain!" And new stores also paste up couplets saying, "May business flourish to the four seas, and wealth abound to the three rivers." Those building houses also stick red paper saying, "The erection of the pillar auspiciously coincides with the fortunate day, and the raising of the beam happily meets the auspicious star." Every undertaking must begin with good fortune. Even the most civilized Westerners find it hard to break away from this kind of superstition. The launching of a ship and the naming of an airplane must involve a delicate beauty holding a bottle of champagne, throwing it with her slender hand, the wine spraying everywhere, and the crowd cheering, wishing it future victory and good luck. In the past, foreigners played this game, but now it has spread to our noble country. If you don't believe me, look at how nowadays when ships are launched and planes are named, it's always some Mrs. So-and-so or socialite throwing champagne, but never the old practice of burning incense and praying. This is progress in our etiquette!

Speaking of champagne, authentic champagne is of course French, costing several dollars a bottle. With a loud bang, it is thrown at the bow of the ship or the nose of the plane, with not even half a drop reaching the mouth. How could Li Bai not complain, and Ruan Ji roll his eyes, repeatedly saying, "What a sin! What a sin! What a pity! What a pity!" Recently, at the naming ceremony of the Hangzhou airplane, newspapers reported that everything else was the same, except that Shaoxing wine was used instead of champagne, which was quite novel. Some people said that Shaoxing wine is a domestic product, which promotes national goods. Some people said that Shaoxing wine is only a few cents a bottle, which promotes thrift. I don't agree with either of these points. As for promoting national goods, the airplane itself is from abroad, so why bother about a bottle of foreign wine? As for promoting thrift, such a large sum of money has already been given to foreigners, so why fuss about the price of a bottle of wine?

There was a follower of the altar who was truly filial. He thought that Buddhist teachings were boundless, and because he deeply missed his deceased mother, he prayed to the altar spirit to allow him to see the face of his departed mother. After a while, the altar spirit descended, instructing him to wait for an opportunity, and he would receive an edict in response during the next descent.

The disciples and believers below the altar were stirred by these words, and everyone hoped to catch a glimpse of their deceased relatives. They all knelt before the altar spirit and made the same request, but the altar spirit gave them a clever answer, saying that it would be discussed at the next descent.

The next altar date arrived. A T-shaped wooden stylus was held by two people, jumping east and west, drawing chaotic characters in the sand on the plate. The altar spirit descended, announcing to the crowd, "Only two people have the opportunity to see the faces of their own relatives." It instructed them to go to a certain mountain in Hangzhou on a certain night and photograph the space. Many miracles would surely be discovered.

They followed the instructions of the altar spirit. After the photos were developed, images of figures in ancient attire appeared, resembling the faces of the individuals when they were alive. This further strengthened their faith, and they quickly spread this spiritual phenomenon among themselves.

Friends, have you received the baptism of science? Do you believe that these miracles are not tricks to deceive fools? Friends, do not hesitate, and give us a clear judgment!

The thing is a foreign product, the ceremony is Western, and it's mixed with some local wine. What does that amount to? In the past, Zigong wanted to get rid of the sacrificial sheep, but Confucius was furious, pointing his finger and scolding, "You are a petty miser! You're being stingy with a sheep, but I want to maintain the ritual!" This time, the people of Hangzhou used Shaoxing wine. If Confucius were alive today, he definitely wouldn't approve.

I have come up with a good idea: the name of champagne should not be abolished. Speculating liquor companies can invent a type of national product champagne specifically for throwing bottles. It can be filled with cold water or Shaoxing wine, since it's going to be thrown away anyway.

If one day China builds its own airplanes and warships, and then uses Shaoxing wine for the bottle-throwing ceremony, using entirely domestic products, then I would have no choice but to approve.

China in Water and Fire 248

— Yu Youqing

Our China really has a relationship with water and fire. During the restoration in the Xinhai year, there was once a flood. At that time, you were still a primary school student, eating at a square table, I still remember. The year before last, there was another big flood, and at the same time, the Northeast was filled with gunfire, the heartbreaking September 18th Incident. During the Battle of Shanghai, Zhabei once again became a place of bombardment. This year, there is the Yellow River breach flood. From atop Kaifeng city, one can see the water scenery. On the Bund and Nanjing Road in Shanghai, one can travel by small gasoline boat. Besides these things, further back in time, there were the Zhili-Fengtian Wars and the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Wars, which bestowed upon the people no small amount of gunfire. Not long after, the two Lius in Sichuan fought fiercely, giving the people a taste of fire. The very secret and semi-public troops of Liu Zhennian set fires wildly in a certain county of Zhejiang, also giving the people a taste of fire, because they had never seen gunfire, so they switched to setting fires. In the summer, Shanghai shows off its water skills in the swimming pools. When it gets cold, they squat by the stove, not wanting to leave for a moment. Young people love to smoke opium, bowing to the fire, and when they are idle, they snatch snake-like women and jump around wildly like sailors. Alas, broken China, unable to escape the fate of water and fire, we are in deep water and scorching fire. Do we not want to leave it? Roar! People of China, stop being water ghosts and fire monsters.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 249

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 17: Who Can Be Heartless When Thinking of Home? Exhausted Soldiers; Warfare Never Tires of Deceit, Heroic Words Strengthen the Army's Resolve

Zhao Ziqiang collapsed onto the bed, his legs spread apart. At the same time, he clapped his hands and threw them outwards, sighing, "How are we supposed to do this? The company is only borrowing thirty dollars for the departure." Guan Yaowu laughed, "You're taking things too seriously, that's why you can't find a solution. Actually, we don't need to worry so much. Just treat it as if we're still stationed in Xiyuan and haven't left yet. That way, we won't need to spend any money." Zhao Ziqiang said, "Unlike you, you have a family. Don't you need to prepare some settlement money?" Guan Yaowu said, "If you think like that, there's no end to it. If we get to a place with postal services and get paid, I'll send money home to them. If we get to a place without postal services, they'll just have to accept their fate and endure it. Anyway, not many people will starve to death in this world." Zhao Ziqiang forced a smile, "If you think like that, then indeed, there's nothing that can't be solved. But I can't think like that. I only have a sixty-year-old father left at home. How can I let him endure it?" Guan Yaowu shook his head with a smile, "It's not just for that, is it? You also have someone special in your heart, don't you?" Zhao Ziqiang sighed, "Hey! Don't mention it." He clasped the ten fingers of his two hands tightly together, lowered his head, almost touching his chest. The depression and oppression in his heart that he couldn't express were even more severe than Guan Yaowu's. In the room, one person sat on the bed, and the other stood leaning against a small table. Both of them were silent. After a long time, Guan Yaowu suddenly raised his head and said, "Old brother, don't think about it. Once it's over, it's over. We just leave and don't care if the sky falls. Then it's no problem. Let's go back to the company and take care of things. Don't overthink it." As he spoke, he walked over and lightly patted Zhao Ziqiang on the shoulder a few times. He had been silent for a long time. Finally, he straightened up suddenly, stood up, and said, "Okay, I trust you." As he spoke, he sighed again before turning back to the company headquarters. As he went downstairs from here, he passed under Yin Deren's room and heard a faint sound of opera singing coming from the window, "Brother Yue, he treats me like a brother. The World's Biggest Pig 252

A man named Chebier in Tennessee, USA, has hundreds of pigs on his farm. Among them is a pig weighing about 2,500 pounds (about 1,560 kilograms) and 8 feet 7 inches long, the largest pig in the world. He can produce an average of three such large pigs each year to supply the market.

Diplomacy Triggered by a Chicken 253

Relations between Yugoslavia and Bulgaria have recently been very strained. A few days ago, a chicken almost caused a major diplomatic problem. One day, the cook in the headquarters of the Yugoslav border guard wanted to kill a chicken for cooking. When he went to catch a few chickens in the garden, the chickens ran wildly and escaped outside the garden. The cook chased after them with a knife and unknowingly crossed the border into Bulgarian territory. When the Bulgarian guards were not looking, the cook caught a chicken and was about to escape back when he was spotted by Bulgarians, who reported it to the government. The Bulgarian government then lodged a serious protest, which was peacefully resolved after Yugoslavia apologized.
